### [39] [Luminosity functions and IMF variations from large samples of HII regions and molecular clouds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18883)
*Jonathan Braine,Edvige Corbelli*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用本地星系中HII区和巨分子云（GMC）的大样本数据，比较CO与Hα光度函数，并通过数值模拟检验恒星形成是否依赖于母云质量，结果未发现最大恒星质量随云或星团质量变化的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究HII区与母GMC之间的关联，特别是大质量恒星是否只在大质量GMC中形成，以及最大恒星质量是否随云质量变化。

Method: 比较CO（代表GMC质量分布）和Hα（代表电离恒星辐射）光度函数；结合Salpeter、Kroupa和Chabrier初始质量函数（IMF），利用恒星质量-光度-半径关系，数值计算年轻星团的总光度和Hα辐射；假设星团质量为母云质量的固定比例（3%），并考虑完全随机IMF情形。

Result: CO光度函数始终比Hα光度函数更陡，且两者在外盘均变陡；在观测极限内（无法探测小分子云和低光度HII区），未发现最大恒星质量随GMC或星团质量变化的证据。

Conclusion: 观测和模型均不支持‘极大质量恒星仅在大质量云或星团中形成’的观点；恒星形成可能在各类质量的GMC中以相似方式发生。

Abstract: Large high-quality samples of HII regions and their parent Giant Molecular Clouds (GMC) are now available for local galaxies. It is therefore possible to investigate links between the CO and H$α$ luminosity functions and whether massive stars form in GMCs of all masses. The CO luminosity functions (LF), representing the distribution of GMC masses, are consistently steeper than the H$α$ luminosity functions. The CO LF invariably steepens in the outer disk where fewer massive GMCs are present beyond the median cloud galactocentric distance. The H$α$ LF also steepens in the outer disk for most of the galaxies examined. Using Salpeter, Kroupa, and Chabrier Initial Mass Functions (IMF) along with stellar mass-luminosity-radius relations, we compute numerically the bolometric luminosity and H$α$ emission from young star clusters. The cluster masses are linked to the GMC mass by assuming that the cluster mass is a constant fraction (3\%) of the parent cloud mass. In particular, results for a fully stochastic IMF are compared to suggestions that very massive stars only form in massive clusters or clouds. Within the limits of the observations -- no small molecular clouds or low-luminosity HII regions can be detected at the typical $\sim 10$~Mpc distance of the sample galaxies -- we find no evidence for a maximum stellar mass which varies with cloud or cluster mass.

</details>


### [40] [Variations in the 6.2 $μ$m polycyclic aromatic hydrocarbon band in Active Galactic Nuclei- and Starburst-dominated galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18901)
*Carla M. Canelo,Dinalva A. Sales,Vitor Avelaneda,Alexander G. G. M. Tielens,Miriani Pastoriza,Amâncio C. S. Friaça*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文分析了175个来自IDEOS数据库星系的6.2 μm多环芳烃（PAH）谱带，依据Peeters分类法将其分为A、B、C三类；发现80%样本属A类，可能暗示含氮PAH存在；同时考察了6.0 μm水冰吸收及6.3 μm后次级谱特征的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解星暴（SB）与活动星系核（AGN）环境中多环芳烃（PAHs）的分布与特性，特别是其在星际介质中的作用及受中心辐射和尘埃结构影响的机制。

Method: 对175个IDEOS数据库星系的SB、AGN及混合主导光谱中6.2 μm PAH谱带进行拟合，并按Peeters分类法（基于峰位）划分为A/B/C类；同时分析6.0 μm水冰吸收及6.3 μm后的次级谱特征影响。

Result: 80%样本属于Peeters A类（峰位蓝移），可能反映含氮PAH；水冰吸收对6.2 μm PAH带影响微弱；10个星系在6.3 μm后出现显著次级谱特征；引入双组分拟合后，主PAH峰普遍蓝移并归为A类。

Conclusion: PAH谱形在SB与AGN环境中呈现系统性差异，A类主导提示可能存在氮掺杂PAH；次级谱特征及拟合方法显著影响分类结果，需进一步研究以厘清不同星系环境中PAH的物理化学演化。

Abstract: Polycyclic aromatic hydrocarbons (PAHs) are fundamental to understanding the interstellar medium (ISM) of several astrophysical objects. Normally present in Starburst (SB) galaxies, they have also been more frequently detected in active galaxy nuclei (AGNs), suggesting an inner dusty torus that can shield the radiation from the central black role. In this work, we analyze the 6.2 $μ$m PAH band of SB-, AGN- and mixed-dominated spectra from 175 IDEOS database galaxies. After fitting of the band, the sources were distributed into the Peeters' A, B and C classes according to their profile peak positions. Class A objects are predominant in 80% of the entire sample, which could indicate the presence of PAHs with nitrogen incorporation. The water ice absorption at 6.0 $μ$m was also studied in eleven objects, and it affected the PAH band poorly. A prominent second spectral feature after 6.3 $μ$m is present in ten galaxies. Fitting both PAH profiles at 6.2 $μ$m changes all the fit results: the first profile is consistently blue-shifted and classified as class A due to the presence of the second component. Further studies are needed to better comprehend these PAH trends in galactic environments.

### [41] [Interaction-induced HI gas concentration with centrally-enhanced star formation in ALFALFA-SDSS galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18926)
*Yanhan Guo,Cheng Li*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用ALFALFA和SDSS大样本星系数据，统计分析了星系相互作用对中性氢（HI）气体中心集中度及其中心恒星形成增强的影响，发现潮汐相互作用在统计上同步驱动HI中心集中与中心恒星形成增强，且气体集中是恒星形成增强的必要条件（极小分离除外）；环境（如中心/伴星系角色）显著调控该过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解星系相互作用如何影响中性氢气体分布及其与恒星形成活动的关系，特别是中心区域的物理耦合机制。

Method: 基于ALFALFA和SDSS约10^4个星系样本，采用HI谱线参数K（表征气体集中度）和比恒星形成率（sSFR），结合成对星系的增强函数及邻近环境统计（如小尺度伴星系概率、聚类强度），分析HI浓度与sSFR增强随投影距离的演化关系。

Result: 1) HI更集中或sSFR更高的星系在<100h^{-1}kpc尺度上邻近伴星系概率更高、聚类更强，尤其在低质量星系中显著；2) HI浓度与sSFR增强在相互作用过程中呈现统计同步性；3) 气体中心集中是中心恒星形成增强的必要条件（极小分离除外）；4) 中心星系相比卫星星系在气体分数、气体集中度和sSFR增强上均更强。

Conclusion: 潮汐相互作用在统计意义上同步驱动HI气体中心集中与中心恒星形成增强，气体集中是恒星形成触发的关键前置条件，且环境（中心/卫星角色）起重要调节作用。

Abstract: We present a statistical analysis for the interaction-induced central concentration of HI gas distributions and its connection with interaction-induced central star formation enhancement, using a large sample of $\sim 10^4$ galaxies from the ALFALFA and SDSS surveys. By adopting the HI profile parameter $K$, an indicator of gas concentration inferred from the integrated 21 cm emission line, we find that galaxies with more centrally concentrated HI (higher $K$ values) or enhanced specific star foramtion rate (sSFR) exhibit significantly stronger clustering and higher probability of hosting a nearby neighbor on scales below $100h^{-1}\mathrm{kpc}$, which is more pronounced in low-mass galaxies. Furthermore, by utilizing the enhancement functions for a sample of galaxy pairs, we directly trace the evolution of HI concentration and sSFR enhancement as a function of projected separation. Our findings indicate that tidal interactions drive a statistical synchrony between the central concentration of atomic gas and the enhancement of central star formation. Gas concentration appears to be a necessary condition for central star formation enhancement in interacting systems at all but the smallest separations. Compared to satellite galaxies, central galaxies exhibit stronger enhancement of gas fraction, gas concentration and sSFR, suggesting the role of environmental regulation.

### [42] [HECATEv2: An all-sky galaxy catalogue for multimessenger astrophysics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18970)
*E. Kyritsis,A. Zezas,K. Kovlakas,C. Daoutis,K. Kouroumpatzakis,A. Hornschemeier,A. Basu-Zych*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: HECATEv2 是一个升级版的全天域星系目录，包含约20.5万个邻近星系（v<14000 km/s），在距离框架、多波段测光、质量参数（如恒星质量、恒星形成率、金属丰度）、活动星系核分类及黑洞质量等方面实现了显著提升与标准化，是研究本地宇宙中星系-黑洞关联、暂现源宿主及特殊星系的重要参考目录。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为提供更准确、全面且标准化的本地宇宙星系参数，支持星系演化、SMBH-宿主关系、引力波/高能暂现源宿主识别等前沿研究，需对初版HECATE目录进行系统性升级。

Method: 基于HyperLEDA数据库构建相同样本（204733个v<14000 km/s星系），引入新宇宙学距离框架；融合SDSS-DR17/NSA、PS1-DR2和AllWISE数据实现光学至中红外测光扩展与均一化；新增质量参数（SFR、Mstar、金属丰度、AGN分类、BH质量）推导方法，并加入多重质量控制标志（恒星污染、测光异常、坐标不一致）。

Result: >70%星系具备SFR与Mstar，~90%具金属丰度，>50%具活动分类，~86%具黑洞质量；提供空间完备性图；在LB、LKs、SFR、Mstar等关键参数上，是光谱红移完备性最高的本地宇宙目录之一。

Conclusion: HECATEv2凭借其广度、深度与参数一致性，成为本地宇宙多维星系研究的基准目录，在覆盖范围和参数完整性上优于或媲美GLADE+、NED-LVS等主流目录。

Abstract: We present HECATEv2, the second release of the Heraklion Extragalactic Catalogue (HECATE), an all-sky, value-added galaxy catalogue comprising 204733 galaxies from the HyperLEDA database with recession velocity <14000 km/s (D~200 Mpc). This release focuses on qualitative upgrades of the provided information while maintaining the same parent galaxy sample as HECATEv1. Improvements include a new cosmology-based distance framework, expanded and homogenised optical and mid-infrared photometry from SDSS-DR17/NSA, PS1-DR2, and AllWISE, and new quality-control flags for stellar contamination, incorrect photometry, and coordinate inconsistencies. We also extend the galaxy-size coverage and derive stellar population parameters for a substantially larger fraction of the sample. Star-formation rates (SFR) and stellar masses (Mstar) are now available for >70% of galaxies using updated mid-IR/optical calibrations that account for stellar population age and dust attenuation, while gas-phase metallicities are derived for ~90%. Activity classifications are provided for >50% of galaxies based on spectroscopic and/or photometric diagnostics, and supermassive black hole masses for ~86%. In terms of L$_{B}$,L$_{Ks}$,SFR, and Mstar, HECATEv2 is among the most complete local-Universe catalogues with spectroscopic redshifts. We also provide spatial completeness maps as a function of distance and luminosity, highlighting variations across the sky. Compared to other catalogues (e.g. GLADE+, NED-LVS), HECATEv2 offers broader (optical, near- and far-IR photometry, metallicity, activity classifications) or comparable (mid-IR photometry, SFR, Mstar) coverage, making it a robust reference for studies of SMBH-host galaxy connections, gravitational-wave and high-energy transient hosts, population analyses, and rare galaxy subpopulations.

Conclusion: 光谱后随是高效甄别卫星的关键手段；当前样本近乎完备覆盖大质量卫星；低质量宿主（如LMC/SMC质量星系）对卫星的熄火存在中等强度影响，填补了孤立星系与MW类宿主之间的演化空白。

Abstract: We present results from our ongoing campaign to follow up the satellite candidates from the Identifying Dwarfs of MC Analog GalaxiEs (ID-MAGE) survey. Previously, we published a list of 355 unresolved satellite candidates identified around 36~nearby LMC- and SMC-mass hosts (D$=$4$-$10~Mpc). We present the velocities of 83 satellite candidates from new Green Bank Telescope \hi\ observations, optical long-slit spectra, and the Dark Energy Survey Instrument Data Release 1. Based on their velocities, we identify six candidates as probable satellite galaxies ($6.5\times10^5\leq M_\star/M_\odot\leq1.5\times10^7$) and 77 as background galaxies. Our results underscore the ability of spectroscopic follow-up to effectively separate satellites from background galaxies. Using the refined sample, we update our previously derived estimates for the average satellite population per host and find 1.7$\pm$0.7 (1.0$\pm$0.3) satellites per LMC-mass (SMC-mass) host. Our current satellite sample includes 25 galaxies confirmed by distances or velocities. This set includes the complete satellite populations of three hosts (UGC~04422: zero satellites, UGC~08201: zero satellites, NGC~3432: four satellites), which we compare to simulations and known satellite systems from the literature. Our sample is nearly complete for the most massive satellites (M$_\star > 10^7~M_\odot$). We find these massive satellites have a quenched fraction of 10--25\%, placing them between the $<$5\% quenched fraction of isolated galaxies and the 40--70\% quenched fraction of MW-analog satellites with $10^7~M_\odot < $ M$_\star < 10^8~M_\odot$. This demonstrates the impact that low-mass galaxies have on the evolution of their satellites.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于一致的YSO样本，提取空间分布中的显著小尺度子结构（NESTs）；采用光度分类法确定YSO演化等级（如0/I类），并统计分析各类YSO在NESTs及整体区域中的分布特征。

Result: 发现高近期恒星形成活动区域中，多数NESTs具有更高活动水平；NESTs中高活性比例随区域整体活动增强而上升；约一半区域中NESTs内存在显著的演化阶段跨度，反映星形成梯度或阶段性；NESTs在高活性区中表现为原始形成遗迹，凸显碎裂作用。

Abstract: We provide the community with a homogeneous catalogue of small, significant substructures (henceforth NESTs) extracted from the spatial distribution of Young Stellar Objects (YSOs) in a large, consistent sample of star-forming regions. The catalog allows us to explore the relevance of small scale spatial substructure and discuss the interpretation of NESTs as tracers of star formation activity and remnants of the star formation process. We apply our procedure to consistent catalogues of YSOs to obtain NESTs in a sample of star-forming regions. We apply a photometric classification scheme to obtain the evolutionary stage of YSOs and statistically explore the distribution of class 0/I objects as a proxy of recent star formation activity. The region sample is diverse (in distance, size, structure, and global evolutionary stage), and we consequently find different structural properties and star formation histories. Most NESTs in regions with high recent star formation activity show even higher levels of activity. Moreover, the proportion of NESTs with higher activity than the region average increases with the global level of activity of the region. In approximately half of the regions we also find significant spans in the evolutionary stages of the NESTs, consistent with gradients and episodes of star formation. The combination of NESTs with a statistical exploration of the star formation history within each region provides robust and powerful insights into the star formation process. Our results support the role of NESTs as pristine remnants of star formation in highly active regions,stressing the role of fragmentation. The combination of small structures with large scale spatio-evolutionary patterns suggests hyerarchical, prolonged, dynamic, and complex star formation scenarios.

### [45] [Identifying AGNs from X-ray detections---I: Metallicity calibrations in AGNs with X-ray luminosity as the primary input parameter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19181)
*Mark Armah,O. L. Dors,Rogério Riffel,M. V. Cardaci,G. F. Hägele,Rogemar A. Riffel,J. M. Vílchez*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个基于X射线光度（而非电离参数U）的AGN半经验强线金属丰度标定方法，改进了N2和O3N2光学诊断指标，显著降低了系统偏差，精度达~0.2 dex。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统AGN金属丰度标定依赖难以直接观测的电离参数U，导致系统性偏差；本文旨在利用可直接观测的X射线光度L_X构建更可靠、物理意义更明确的标定关系。

Method: 基于Cloudy程序构建大范围光电离模型网格，并与BASS巡天中Seyfert星系的观测数据比对；系统分析AGN光谱指数α_ox、窄线区气体密度N_e、蓝包峰值温度T_BB及X射线光度L_X对N2和O3N2指标的影响。

Result: 建立了适用于8.0≲log(O/H)≲9.1（即0.2≲Z/Z⊙≲2.6）的N2和O3N2新标定关系，1σ精度分别为0.22 dex和0.20 dex；发现L_X对二者存在强且相反的二级依赖，忽略L_X将引入最高达~1.0 dex的金属丰度误差。

Conclusion: 引入X射线光度L_X作为关键参数可有效校正AGN窄线区金属丰度诊断中的系统偏差，为研究AGN化学增丰历史提供更精确的工具。

Abstract: We present the first semi-empirical strong-line calibrations to determine metallicity in Active Galactic Nuclei (AGNs) that use the directly observable X-ray luminosity ($Ł_{\rm X}$) instead of the dimensionless ionization parameter ($U$). The calibrations are derived from an extensive grid of photoionization models computed with the {\sc Cloudy} code, which are compared with observational data of Seyfert nuclei from the Burst Alert Telescope (BAT) AGN Spectroscopic Survey (BASS). In this first paper, we develop new calibrations for two key optical metallicity diagnostics based on the $N2$ and $O3N2$ indices, which are valid in a metallicity range of $8.0 \lesssim \logOH \lesssim 9.1\, {\rm or}\, 0.2 \lesssim (Z/Z_{\odot}) \lesssim 2.6$, with precision of $1σ\approx 0.22$ dex ($N2$) and $\approx 0.20$ dex ($O3N2$). We systematically investigate the influence of the AGN spectral index $(\aox)$, narrow-line region (NLR) gas density (\Ne), the characteristic peak temperature of the Big Blue Bump $(T_{\rm BB})$, and $Ł_{\rm X}$. We find a strong, opposing secondary dependence on $Ł_{\rm X}$ for both indices. We demonstrate that neglecting this parameter overlooks systematic offsets intrinsic to the diagnostics, leading to metallicity errors of up to $\sim 1.0$ dex, particularly for the least and most luminous sources. This framework offers a more precise characterization of chemical enrichment in the NLRs of AGNs by leveraging their intrinsic X-ray emission to mitigate these systematic biases.

### [46] [The structure and evolution of the Galactic high-$α$ disc I. Chemical and age orbital cartography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19230)
*Furkan Akbaba,Danny Horta,Olcay Plevne*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示银河系高α盘的形成历史与结构演化，检验其是否保留早期组装的‘化石记录’，并比较其与低α盘的化学-轨道及年龄-轨道关系。

Method: 基于LAMOST-Gaia数据中具有精确年龄、元素丰度和六维相空间信息的亚巨星样本，构建高α盘在轨道作用量（actions）和角动量坐标下的[Fe/H]、[α/Fe]和年龄分布图；按单丰度星群分别分析，测量化学丰度-轨道与年龄-轨道梯度。

Result: 高α盘在轨道空间中展现出比现时运动学空间更显著、更陡峭的[Fe/H]、[α/Fe]和年龄梯度；其年龄与化学梯度趋势与低α盘定性相似但斜率更平缓；该有序结构表明高α盘结构得以保存，未被后续并合事件完全抹除。

Conclusion: 银河系高α盘主要通过‘由内向外、由下向上’的方式形成，并在经历后期并合后仍保留了早期形成的化学-轨道与年龄-轨道结构，即其具备完整的‘化石记录’。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive chemical and age orbital cartography of the Galactic high-$α$ disc using subgiant stars with precise ages, element abundances, and full phase-space information from the \textsl{LAMOST--Gaia} data set. Specifically, we map how average [Fe/H], [$α$/Fe], and age vary across present-day kinematic and orbital coordinates. We analyse the data in full and across mono-abundance populations to measure element abundance-orbital and age-orbital gradients across orbital actions and angular-momenta. Our results show that the high-$α$ disc exhibits clear and coherent gradients in [Fe/H], [$α$/Fe], and age with orbits; these gradients are much stronger and sharper in orbital space than in present-day kinematics, showing that orbital diagnostics recover the intrinsic disc structure of old disc populations more effectively than instantaneous kinematic coordinates. We find that older high-$α$ populations display qualitatively similar element abundance--orbital and age--orbital trends to stars in the low-$α$ disc, although the high-$α$ gradients are generally shallower. The presence of these ordered correlations indicates that the old high-$α$ disc is structured, and preserved a strong fossil record of its early assembly despite the Milky Way's subsequent accretion history. This result implies that later mergers did not fully erase the chemical-orbital and age-orbital structure imprinted during the high-$α$ disc's earliest formation epoch. All together, these findings indicate that the Galactic high-$α$ disc formed mainly through inside-out and upside-down growth.

</details>

### [47] [More on near-horizon charges black holes with gravitational hair in three dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18072)
*Seyed Naseh Sajadi,Supakchai Ponglertsakul,Julio Oliva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统地修订并推广了协变相空间方法，适用于包含最高四次黎曼张量项的任意维高曲率引力理论，并将其应用于旋转BTZ黑洞近视界渐近对称性与荷的计算，成功恢复第一热力学定律；同时将含引力毛发黑洞（如新质量引力）的近视界电荷计算扩展至R^4阶。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 延续高曲率引力中近视界电荷的研究，寻找具有普适行为的理论扇区，特别是面向弦论α'修正（如Type II中α'^3 R^4项）及具引力毛发黑洞（如New Massive Gravity）的微观熵解释需求。

Method: 采用协变相空间方法，推导适用于任意维度、含至R^4项的广义引力理论的规范不变电荷与渐近对称性公式，并应用于旋转BTZ与New Massive Gravity中的静态/旋转毛发黑洞近视界几何。

Result: 1) 给出任意维、至R^4阶高曲率引力的协变相空间通用公式；2) 在旋转BTZ中一致重现黑洞热力学第一定律；3) 首次将New Massive Gravity中毛发黑洞的近视界电荷计算推广至R^4精度；4) 明确给出各类广义拉氏量的显式表达式（见附录）。

Conclusion: 协变相空间方法可稳健推广至高阶曲率理论，近视界电荷结构在R^4阶仍保持普适性与一致性，为高曲率引力和弦论低能有效理论中的黑洞熵与对称性研究提供了可靠框架。

Abstract: With the aim of continuing the exploration of near-horizon charges in higher-curvature gravity, searching for sectors leading to universal behaviors, we first provide a thorough revision and formulae of the covariant phase-space method applied to arbitrary gravitational theories containing up to quartic terms in the Riemann tensor in arbitrary dimension. These results can be applied in diverse setups, in particular in the context of $α'$ corrections to String Theory, where it is known that in Type II theories, the first correction to the Einstein-Hilbert Lagrangian goes as $α'^3 \mathcal{R}^4$. Then, we test these formulae for near horizon asymptotic symmetries of the rotating BTZ spacetime where the first law of black hole thermodynamics is consistently recovered. It was recently realized that a subset of these higher curvature gravities do admit black holes with gravitational hair, whose entropy can be microscopically accounted for, as is the case of New Massive Gravity. In this case, the four maximally symmetric vacua of the theory coincide, and the theory acquires an extra gauge symmetry when linearized around such a vacuum. We study the near-horizon asymptotic symmetries and compute the associated charges, both in the static and rotating hairy black holes, extending up to $\mathcal{R}^4$, a work that was previously done only up to a quadratic term. In order to allow for a continuous lecture on the work, we report the explicit expressions of the general Lagrangians in the appendices.

</details>

Result: 证明Spavieri等人的主张不成立，Wang等人的实验并未否定狭义相对论。

Conclusion: Spavieri等人的批评基于逻辑谬误，狭义相对论中的相对同时性依然成立。

Abstract: In this comment, we demonstrate that the claim by Spavieri et al., asserting that Wang et al.'s interferometric experiment disproves the special theory of relativity by revealing that simultaneity must be an absolute concept independent of the observer's state of motion, is based on circular reasoning and therefore constitutes a logical fallacy.

TL;DR: 本文探讨了将SU(N)对称性与引力场在四维弯曲洛伦兹时空中的耦合问题，推广了之前SU(3)耦合的工作，并引入新四维标架（tetrads）以构建大统一场论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着夸克物理发展（如引入奇异数、粲数等新量子数），需将对称群从SU(3)推广至SU(N)（如SU(4)），进而实现引力与内禀对称性的统一描述。

Method: 借鉴SU(3)×SU(2)×U(1)情形，引入新型四维标架（tetrads），并证明其相关局部规范群与标架变换群张量积之间的同构性定理。

Result: 建立了SU(N)对称性与引力场在四维弯曲洛伦兹时空中的耦合形式，揭示了局部对称群与标架变换群之间的深刻几何联系。

Conclusion: 该工作为四维弯曲时空中的大统一场论提供了新的几何框架，支持将粒子物理标准模型对称性自然嵌入引力理论中。

Abstract: The discovery of the SU(3) symmetry was fundamental as to establishing an ordering principle in particle physics. We already studied how to couple the SU(3) symmetry to the gravitational field in four-dimensional curved Lorentzian spacetimes. The multiplets of equal quantum numbers are translated through natural elements in Riemannian geometry into local multiplets of equal gravitational field. As quark physics developed since the seventies, it was necessary to incorporate new symmetries to the models, that ensued in the incorporation of new quantum numbers like Charm, for example. Charm is an additive quantum number like isospin T3 and hypercharge Y and the standard T3-Y diagrams were extended onto another third axis. Then, instead of the fundamental triplet we have a quartet {u; d; s; c} as the smallest representation of the symmetry group, leading to the introduction of SU(4) as the new group of symmetries. In this paper we will not restrict ourselves exclusively to the symmetry group SU(4) and we will set out to analyze the coupling of the SU(N) symmetry to the gravitational field. To this end new tetrads will be introduced as we did for the SU(3) x SU(2) x U(1) case. These tetrads have outstanding properties that enable these constructions. New theorems will be proved regarding the isomorphic nature of these local symmetry gauge groups and tensor products of groups of local tetrad transformations. This is a paper about grand field uni?fication in four-dimensional curved Lorentzian spacetimes.

### [50] [The Steep Price of No Hair in Thiemann Regularized Loop Quantum Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18175)
*Meysam Motaharfar,Parampreet Singh*

Main category: gr-qc

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清和重新诠释Gan等人关于Thiemann正则化圈量子宇宙学中各向异性剪切被普遍压制这一现象的起源及其适用范围。

Method: 分析Thiemann正则化下Bianchi-I各向异性时空的圈量子宇宙学模型，考察其普朗克尺度行为、各向异性剪切演化及经典性恢复条件。

Result: 发现存在一个涌现的普朗克尺度德西特相，能自然压制各向异性剪切并导致各向同化，但该机制非普适，且宇宙在后反弹阶段虽达宏观尺度却始终无法真正经典化。

Conclusion: Gan等人所发现的各向异性剪切压制机制确有其量子引力根源，但其有效性受限于模型细节，并不具普适性；该机制不能保证宇宙最终回归经典，需谨慎解读其物理含义。

Abstract: Loop quantum cosmology based on Thiemann's regularization procedure leads to the resolution of the big bang singularity and bounce in the isotropic setting. A key distinction from standard loop quantum cosmology is that, in this framework, either the pre-bounce or post-bounce epoch is necessarily characterized by an emergent Planckian de Sitter phase. In this work we explore the Planckian physics of Thiemann regularized loop quantization of the Bianchi-I spacetimes. We show that as in the isotropic model, there exists an emergent de Sitter phase which naturally dampens anisotropic shear and removes cosmic hair. However, this isotropization comes at a steep price: although a macroscopic post-bounce regime is achieved, the universe never becomes truly classical. We further demonstrate that this isotropization mechanism is non-generic. These results help clarify and reinterpret recent results by Gan et al. [1] that, in anisotropic Thiemann regularized loop quantum cosmology, quantum gravity effects generically damp anisotropic shear in a way that is independent of initial conditions and the matter content, and that this anisotropic shear damping mechanism arises from a novel quantum gravity effect. Our work explains the origin of this mechanism and its limitations.

### [51] [Robinson-Trautman spacetimes in (2+1) dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18209)
*Alberto Saa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在(2+1)维时空中保留四维Robinson-Trautman结构特征的演化模型，基于一个含宇宙常数和零流体源的非定态度规，通过单个正函数P(u,φ)完全确定，并引入一个类Calabi流的四阶保长演化方程，数值结果表明其趋向于负宇宙常数下的 boosted BTZ 黑洞稳态解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受四维中面积保持Calabi流作用的启发，构建一个能描述低维引力中由零辐射驱动的耗散动力学的简化玩具模型，并探索其与真实引力辐射现象的结构相似性。

Method: 基于一个已知的含宇宙常数和零流体的精确度规族，选取非定态几何；将度规由单函数P(u,φ)表征；引入一个保长度的四阶演化方程（类Calabi流）来驱动P的演化；通过数值求解验证其向稳态解的弛豫行为。

Result: 该四阶演化方程的稳态解对应于负宇宙常数下的boosted BTZ黑洞；数值模拟显示，任意规则初值P(0,φ)均强烈趋向该稳态解；所构造系统成为描述低维引力中零辐射耗散动力学的简洁有效模型。

Conclusion: 该(2+1)维Robinson-Trautman类演化成功复现了高维关键结构，为研究引力辐射相关现象提供了可控的低维类比框架。

Abstract: We propose a Robinson-Trautman evolution in $(2+1)$-dimensional spacetime that retains key structural features of the four-dimensional case. We consider a recently studied exact family of metrics to select a nonstationary geometry with a cosmological constant, sourced by a null fluid. The metric is completely determined by a single positive function $P(u,φ)$, while the corresponding matter content is encoded in a null-fluid density. Motivated by the role of the area-preserving Calabi flow in four dimensions, we introduce a fourth-order length-preserving evolution equation for $P(u,φ)$ whose stationary configurations correspond, for negative cosmological constant, to boosted BTZ black holes. Numerical solutions strongly support the relaxation of generic regular initial data $P(0,φ)$ toward the stationary sector. The resulting system provides a simple toy model for dissipative dynamics driven by null radiation in lower-dimensional gravity, with several structural similarities to phenomena associated with genuine gravitational radiation.

</details>


### [52] [Holographic Quantum Foam: Theoretical Underpinnings and Observational Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18277)
*Eric Steinbring,Y. Jack Ng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出全息量子泡沫（HQF）理论，指出时空因量子涨落而呈现泡沫状，并预测宇宙中必然存在一个遵循无限统计（量子玻尔兹曼统计）的暗物质组分；该理论与观测定性一致，并利用极端明亮的伽马暴GRB221009A的多波段数据，首次提供了HQF导致遥远点源模糊的潜在观测证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证全息量子泡沫（HQF）理论是否与实验/观测一致，特别是寻找普朗克尺度物理导致遥远点源（如类星体、伽马暴）图像模糊的观测证据。

Method: 基于HQF理论推导其对电磁波前传播的影响，计算真实望远镜观测伽马暴时HQF展宽的点扩散函数（PSF），并结合GRB221009A在光学/近红外、X射线及最高能伽马射线波段的多波段观测数据进行比对分析。

Result: GRB221009A的多波段观测结果与HQF导致的点源模糊预期一致；HQF理论预言的暗 sector 组分遵循无限统计（非费米或玻色统计），且其宇宙学行为与观测定性相符。

Conclusion: HQF理论不仅自洽地统一了量子引力效应与宇宙学观测，还通过GRB221009A这一特殊事件首次获得潜在的观测支持；后续需更多高精度数据进一步检验HQF的定量预测。

Abstract: Spacetime is foamy due to quantum fluctuations. Various gedanken experiments show that distances fluctuate by amounts consistent with the holographic principle, hence the name "holographic quantum foam" (HQF). One important prediction of HQF is that necessarily there exists a dark sector in the universe. The resulting cosmology is found (at least qualitatively) to be consistent with observations. Interestingly the quanta of the dark sector are found not to obey the familiar (fermionic or bosonic) statistics, but the exotic statistics known as infinite statistics (or quantum Boltzmann statistics). The most important challenge now is to check if HQF is consistent with experiments/observations. One way is to look for observational evidence of blurred distant point-sources due to physics at the Planck scale. For over two decades it has been debated whether those tiny inherent uncertainties in time and path-length can accumulate in transiting electromagnetic wavefronts from quasars and Gamma-Ray Bursts (GRBs). But a recent event is special: GRB221009A was extremely bright and energetic. That allowed follow-up across the whole spectrum from the optical/near-infrared through to X-rays, and including the highest-ever-recorded energy gamma-rays; all consistent with blurring by HQF. Those data, and a calculation of the HQF-widened point-spread function (PSF) for real telescopes viewing a GRB are presented.

</details>


### [53] [Contrasting behaviour of two spherically symmetric perfect fluids near a weak null singularity in a spherically symmetric black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18340)
*Raya V. Mancheva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对比了两种球对称物质模型在含弱零曲率奇点（WNS）的球对称时空中的行为：一是球对称尘埃，其能量密度在WNS处有界、无壳交叉；二是刚性完美流体，其能量密度在WNS处发散、速度趋于入射零矢量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验不同物质模型在弱零奇点附近的物理行为差异，以深化对强宇宙监督猜想及奇点处经典广义相对论适用性的理解。

Method: 对尘埃模型采用初值问题分析，证明其速度场保持类时且无壳交叉；对刚性流体模型则通过将其映射为满足线性波方程的标量场，分析其特征初值问题并研究能量密度与速度分量的渐近行为。

Result: 尘埃模型中能量密度有界、速度保持类时、无壳交叉；刚性流体模型中能量密度发散、速度趋近于沿奇点超曲面的入射零矢量。

Conclusion: 不同物质模型在弱零奇点处表现出截然不同的正则性：尘埃保持良好行为，而刚性流体出现发散，表明奇点处的物理行为高度依赖于物质本构关系。

Abstract: In this work we contrast the behaviour of two spherically symmetric matter models in a class of spherically symmetric spacetimes which feature a weak null singularity. This class in particular contains spherically symmetric perturbations of subextremal Reissner-Nordström under the Einstein--Maxwell--scalar field system, a system for which a $C^2$ formulation of the strong cosmic censorship conjecture was proved by Luk-Oh, arXiv:1702.05715 and Dafermos, arXiv:1201.1797. Firstly, we consider the Cauchy problem of spherically symmetric dust falling into the weak null singularity (WNS) where the initial dust velocity is normal to a smooth spacelike curve with certain properties. We prove that the flow of the dust velocity does not experience any shell-crossing before or at the singularity, the velocity vector remains timelike, and that the dust energy density remains bounded as matter approaches the singularity. Secondly, we consider the characteristic initial value problem for stiff perfect fluid falling into the WNS. By relating the stiff fluid velocity and energy density to a scalar field satisfying the homogeneous linear wave equation, we prove that this energy density becomes infinite as we approach the weak null singularity. Furthermore, we show that the ingoing component of the stiff fluid velocity blows up while the outgoing component approaches zero at the singularity. Therefore the velocity vector approaches an ingoing null vector tangent to the singular hypersurface.

</details>


### [54] [Black Hole--Entropy Container or Creator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18374)
*William G Unruh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过线性放大器模型论证黑洞本身不具有熵，但在其运作过程中会创造并发射熵，总发射熵与黑洞质量平方成正比，与传统霍金辐射熵表达式一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建并分析一个不具本征熵但运行中发射熵的线性放大器类比模型，并将其行为与黑洞辐射过程进行对应。

Result: 得出黑洞自身无熵，但能创造并发射熵；总发射熵仍等于标准Bekenstein-Hawking熵（S ∝ M²）。

Conclusion: 黑洞不拥有熵，而是作为熵的产生器，在霍金辐射过程中动态生成并释放熵，从而调和信息悖论与热力学第二定律的表观矛盾。

Abstract: Do black holes possess entropy or do they create it? The dominant assumption is that they possess entropy, and a they evaporate that entropy is emitted and decreases. In this paper I use a model of a linear amplifier, in which I argue that the amplifier has not entropy and yet it emits entropy in the process of it operation. This model is closely related to behaviour of black holes, resulting in answer the question of that title that black holes do not have entropy, but nevertheless them create and emit entropy with the total entropy emitted being the same as the usual expression proportional to the square of the mas of the black hole.

</details>


### [55] [Bosonic and fermionic mutual information of N-partite systems in dilaton black hole background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18439)
*Xiao-Wei Teng,Rui-Yang Xu,Hui-Chen Yang,Shu-Min Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在Garfinkle-Horowitz-Strominger（GHS）稀释子黑洞背景下，自由玻色场和费米场的N体量子关联，重点分析GHZ与W态的多体互信息及相对熵相干性（REC），发现费米互信息大于玻色互信息，而费米REC小于玻色REC；GHZ态互信息大于W态，但REC相反。结果表明，相对论量子信息任务中应依据粒子种类和态结构选择合适量子资源以优化效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究弯曲时空（特别是GHS稀释子黑洞）中不同粒子统计（玻色/费米）和不同纠缠结构（GHZ/W）对多体量子关联（互信息与相干性）的影响，为相对论量子信息提供资源选择依据。

Method: 基于GHS稀释子黑洞背景，对N体GHZ和W态，计算一个观测者位于视界附近、其余在渐近平直区时的多体互信息；通过迹掉视界内不可达模，分别推导玻色场和费米场在该弯曲时空中的解析互信息与相对熵相干性表达式。

Result: 1) 费米场的多体互信息大于玻色场；2) 费米场的相对熵相干性（REC）小于玻色场；3) GHZ态的互信息始终大于W态，而GHZ态的REC小于W态。

Conclusion: 在相对论量子信息任务中，量子资源（粒子类型与纠缠态结构）的选择需针对性优化：费米场更利于互信息相关任务，GHZ态更利于信息共享，W态更利于维持相干性。

Abstract: We investigate multipartite quantum correlations by analyzing the mutual information of N-partite states for both free bosonic and fermionic fields in the background of a Garfinkle-Horowitz-Strominger (GHS) dilaton black hole. Focusing on multipartite GHZ and W states, we examine how the Hawking effect influences the N-partite mutual information when one observer hovers near the event horizon while the remaining observers stay in the asymptotically flat region. By tracing over the inaccessible modes inside the event horizon, we derive analytical expressions for the N-partite mutual information in dilaton spacetime for both bosonic and fermionic fields. Our results show that fermionic mutual information is larger than its bosonic counterpart under the influence of the dilaton black hole, whereas the fermionic relative entropy of coherence (REC) is smaller than the bosonic REC. Moreover, the mutual information of GHZ states is consistently larger than that of W states, while the REC of GHZ states is smaller than that of W states in curved spacetime. These findings indicate that the choice of quantum resources should be tailored to the particle species and state structure in relativistic quantum information tasks to optimize their operational efficiency.

</details>


### [56] [Scalarization of charged Taub-NUT black hole and the entropy bound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18562)
*Lei Zhang,Hai-Shan Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量-高斯-博内引力理论中带电Taub-NUT黑洞的自发标量化现象，发现其无标量背景在特定参数下失稳，产生新的带发黑洞分支，并揭示了其熵的两个普适特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究带电Taub-NUT黑洞在Einstein-Maxwell-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet理论中是否会发生自发标量化，以及标量化后黑洞物理性质（尤其是熵）的变化规律。

Method: 选取合适的耦合函数，使带电Taub-NUT几何成为解析解；分析该无标量背景的线性稳定性；数值求解标量化后的 hairy 黑洞解；系统研究其标量荷、温度与熵等物理量。

Result: 发现标量化解存在一个由电荷和NUT参数张成的二维参数空间；熵具有两个普适特征：(1) 标量化黑洞熵严格大于对应无标量黑洞；(2) 熵在分岔点取得局部极大值，且当电荷固定时，该极大值在一定质量范围内是普适的。

Conclusion: 带电Taub-NUT黑洞可发生自发标量化，生成新的 hairy 解；其熵的普适行为为理解标量化机制及黑洞热力学提供了新线索。

Abstract: We investigate the spontaneous scalarization of charged Taub-NUT black holes within the framework of Einstein-Maxwell-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity. By selecting a suitable coupling function, the theory admits the analytic charged Taub-NUT geometry as a solution. We demonstrate that this scalar-free background becomes unstable within specific parameter regimes, leading to the bifurcation of a new branch of hairy charged Taub-NUT black holes. These solutions are characterized by a two-dimensional parameter space spanned by the electric charge and the NUT parameter. We conduct a systematic study of their properties, specifically the scalar charge, temperature, and entropy. Our analysis reveals that the entropy of the scalarized solutions exhibits particularly compelling features. Two universal characteristics emerge: first, the entropy of the hairy black hole is strictly greater than that of its scalar-free counterpart; second, the entropy reaches a local maximum precisely at the bifurcation point. Notably, when the electric charge is fixed, this maximum entropy value remains universal across a specific range of the mass parameter.

### [57] [Exact pp-wave solutions in shift-symmetric higher-order scalar-tensor theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18794)
*Masato Minamitsuji*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在shift-symmetric二次阶高阶标量-张量（HOST）理论框架下的精确平面前沿引力波（pp波）解，发现满足特定代数条件时其场方程退化为二维拉普拉斯方程，结构上恢复广义相对论真空形式；通过构造特定标量场试探解，得到不扰动时空几何的‘隐形pp波’解，并验证其与Class-Ia DHOST理论的相容性及观测兼容性；进一步分析表明，虽经向形变变换后Brinkmann形式保持，但隐形性质通常丢失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索修改引力理论（特别是DHOST理论）中非线性辐射时空的精确解，检验其与广义相对论的结构相似性、理论自洽性及观测可行性，并理解标量-张量耦合对引力波解的影响。

Method: 基于shift-symmetric二次阶HOST理论，设定pp波度规和特定线性+任意依赖的标量场试探解，推导并简化引力场方程；分析解对DHOST退化条件的满足性；结合当前天文观测约束进行兼容性检验；最后研究该解在向形变变换下的行为。

Result: 1) 在耦合函数满足代数条件时，场方程约化为二维拉普拉斯方程，结构复现GR真空pp波；2) 构造出‘隐形pp波’解：非平凡标量场存在但不改变背景几何；3) 该解满足Class-Ia DHOST退化条件且符合现有观测限制；4) 向形变变换下Brinkmann形式不变，但隐形性一般被破坏。

Conclusion: pp波解在可行的DHOST理论中具有鲁棒性，是研究修改引力中非线性效应的重要工具；‘隐形’特性依赖于特定标量-张量解耦结构，易被更一般的变换破坏。

Abstract: We investigate exact plane-fronted gravitational wave (pp-wave) solutions within the framework of shift-symmetric quadratic-order higher-order scalar--tensor (HOST) theories. These solutions represent fully nonlinear radiative spacetimes that extend beyond the linearized approximation. We demonstrate that under the algebraic conditions on the coupling functions, the gravitational field equations reduce to a two-dimensional Laplace equation for the wave profile, recovering the structural form of vacuum general relativity (GR). By adopting a scalar field ansatz that depends linearly on transverse coordinates and arbitrarily on the retarded null coordinate, we maintain a constant kinetic term of the scalar field. This configuration allows for a \emph{stealth pp-wave} solution, where a nontrivial scalar field profile coexists with the gravitational wave without backreacting on the spacetime geometry. We further show that these stealth configurations are fully compatible with the degeneracy conditions of Class-Ia DHOST theories and satisfy current observational constraints. Finally, we examine the behavior of these solutions under disformal transformations, revealing that while the Brinkmann form is preserved, the stealth property is generically lost due to the mixing of scalar and tensor degrees of freedom. These results establish the robustness of pp-wave solutions in viable DHOST frameworks and highlight their utility for probing nonlinear effects in modified gravity.

</details>


### [58] [Thermodynamics of Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18821)
*Li Hu,Rong-Gen Cai,Shao-Jiang Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson黑洞的热力学性质，通过Christodoulou-Ruffini质量关系定义其守恒质量，解决了因外部电磁场导致的质量计算困难，并验证了第一定律和Smarr公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson黑洞处于非平凡渐近均匀外电磁场中，标准可积性方法无法直接计算其守恒质量，需另寻热力学定义途径。

Method: 采用Christodoulou-Ruffini质量关系作为守恒质量的热力学定义，并据此确定相应生成元，从而消除质量定义的模糊性并构建热力学势。

Result: 成功定义了该黑洞的守恒质量及相关热力学量，所获热力学量自然满足黑洞热力学第一定律和Smarr公式。

Conclusion: Christodoulou-Ruffini质量关系为含外场旋转黑洞提供了合理且自洽的热力学质量定义，拓展了黑洞热力学在非渐近平直时空中的适用性。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic properties of the Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black hole, an exact Petrov type D solution of Einstein-Maxwell theory describing a rotating black hole immersed in an external electromagnetic field. While the conserved angular momentum and electric charge can be computed straightforwardly, the conserved mass cannot be obtained through standard integrability methods due to the nontrivial asymptotically uniform external electromagnetic field. To overcome this difficulty, we adopt the Christodoulou-Ruffini mass relation as a thermodynamic definition of the conserved mass, and identify the associated generator, thereby fixing the ambiguity in defining this conserved mass and constructing the thermodynamic potentials. These thermodynamic quantities naturally satisfy the first law of black-hole thermodynamics as well as the Smarr formula.

</details>

*Zainab Malik*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文推导了嵌入Dehnen型暗物质晕中的渐近平直黑洞的引力准正规模的解析表达式，发现轴向扰动分裂为非等谱的'上'和'下'两个通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究暗物质晕对黑洞准正规模的影响，以探索暗物质环境对引力波信号的可能修正。

Method: 在超越eikonal近似的框架下，利用Dehnen型暗物质晕模型给出的解析度规，推导引力准正规模的解析表达式。

Result: 得到了相对紧凑且准确的准正规模解析表达式，并发现轴向引力扰动分裂为两个非等谱通道（'up'和'down'）。

Conclusion: 暗物质晕的存在显著改变黑洞的准正规模结构，尤其导致轴向扰动失去等谱性，这对引力波天文学中黑洞参数提取具有潜在影响。

Abstract: Using an expansion beyond the eikonal regime, we derive relatively compact and accurate analytic expressions for the gravitational quasinormal modes of an asymptotically flat black hole supported by a Dehnen-type dark-matter halo. The spacetime admits a simple analytic metric describing a supermassive black hole embedded in a galactic environment, with the lapse function $f(r)=1-\frac{2 M r^{2}}{(r+a)^{3}}.$ The parameter $a$ sets the characteristic scale of the surrounding halo and controls the regularization of the central region. The axial gravitational sector splits into two distinct channels, referred to as the "up" and "down" perturbations, which are not isospectral.

</details>


### [60] [Observational Signatures of Rotating Ayón-Beato-García Black Holes: Shadows, Accretion Disks and Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18963)
*Zhenglong Ban,Meng Chen,Rong-Jia Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了旋转Ayón-Beato-García黑洞（含质量M、自旋a和电荷ζ）的阴影、吸积盘及观测图像，发现阴影尺寸随电荷增大而减小，高自旋近极值情况下呈“D”形；吸积盘内边缘延伸至视界，并区分ISCO内外粒子动力学；(a, ζ)与观测倾角共同影响图像不对称性和内阴影畸变；高倾角下出现“帽状”结构；通过对比EHT对M87*和Sgr A*的观测，约束得电荷参数范围0.132811M < ζ < 0.213607M。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解带电旋转黑洞（ABG黑洞）的可观测特征（如阴影与吸积盘图像），并利用EHT观测数据对其物理参数（尤其是电荷ζ）进行实际约束，以检验其作为真实致密天体候选者的可行性。

Method: 基于ABG黑洞度规，数值计算光线追踪以获得阴影轮廓与观测图像；扩展吸积盘至事件视界，区分ISCO内外粒子运动；计算直接光与透镜光的红移分布；结合不同倾角（17°, 50°, 90°）下的理论阴影直径与EHT对M87*和Sgr A*的测量结果，进行参数联合约束。

Result: 阴影尺寸随电荷ζ增加而减小；近极值自旋（a=0.95）下阴影呈'D'形；高倾角导致图像分离形成'帽状'结构；(a, ζ)与倾角共同调制图像不对称性与内阴影畸变；红移分布随参数与视角显著变化；EHT数据联合约束得电荷范围0.132811M < ζ < 0.213607M。

Conclusion: ABG黑洞的阴影与吸积盘图像具有独特可辨识特征，其电荷参数可在当前EHT精度下被有效约束；所得ζ区间同时兼容M87*与Sgr A*观测，支持ABG类带电黑洞作为潜在的天体物理模型。

Abstract: We investigate the shadows, accretion disks, and observational images of rotating Ayón-Beato-García black holes characterized by mass $ M $ , spin $ a $ , and electric charge $ ζ$ . Our analysis reveals that the shadow size decreases with increasing $ ζ$, and in near-extremal configurations (e.g., $ a = 0.95 $), the shadow adopts a distinctive ``D''-shaped morphology. For the accretion disk, we extend its inner edge to the event horizon and account for distinct particle dynamics inside and outside the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO). We find that the correlation between $ (a, ζ) $ and the observer's inclination angle significantly influences image asymmetry and inner shadow distortion. At higher inclinations, the direct and lensed images separate, forming a hat-like structure. Additionally, we compute the redshift distribution of the disk's direct and lensed emissions under varying parameters and viewing angles. By comparing theoretical shadow diameters with the Event Horizon Telescope observations of M87 $^{*}$ and Sgr A $^{*}$--using inclination angles of $17^{\circ} $, $ 50^{\circ} $, and $ 90^{\circ} $--we constrain the viable parameter space, yielding the joint bound $0.132811\,M < ζ< 0.213607\,M$ consistent with both sources.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用特定形式的f(T)函数和H(z)表达式构建两个宇宙学模型；使用χ²最小化为基础的贝叶斯统计方法，分别拟合宇宙时钟（CC）和联合（CC+Pantheon）数据集以确定模型参数；进而分析减速参量、能量密度、压强、暗能量状态方程、能量条件及statefinder诊断等。

Conclusion: 所提出的f(T)模型能合理描述宇宙加速膨胀历史，具备物理自洽性与观测兼容性，为修改引力理论提供了有力候选。

Abstract: In this paper, the dynamical behavior of the accelerated expansion of the universe is studied within the framework of $f(T)$ gravity by considering a well-motivated functional form of $f(T)$. A specific form of the Hubble parameter is assumed, which under two different cases, leads to two distinct cosmological models expressed in terms of the redshift parameter $H(z)$, providing insights into cosmic dynamics. These models are employed to explore the expansion history of the universe and the evolution of several cosmological parameters. Using Bayesian statistical techniques based on the $χ^{2}$-minimization method, the median values of the model parameters are determined for both the cosmic chronometer (CC) and the joint (CC + Pantheon) datasets. The evolution of the deceleration parameter, energy density, pressure and the equation of state parameter for dark energy is analyzed. Additionally, the validity of the energy conditions and the nature of the statefinder diagnostic are examined. The present age of the universe is also estimated for the proposed models.

Zhu,Z. -H. Zhu,A. B. Zimmerman,L. Zimmermann,M. E. Zucker,J. Zweizig*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文是三篇系列论文的第一篇，利用GWTC-4.0中91个高置信度引力波事件，对广义相对论（GR）在强场、动力学区域进行多方面检验，结果未发现显著偏离GR的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA探测器灵敏度持续提升，越来越多高质量引力波信号被探测到，为在强场和动力学条件下严格检验广义相对论提供了前所未有的机会。

Method: 基于GWTC-4.0目录中91个双探测器以上确认、虚警率≤10⁻³ yr⁻¹的引力波事件，开展四类广义相对论一致性检验：残差与噪声一致性、低频/高频推断的并合后最终质量与自旋一致性、次主导多极矩幅度一致性、非GR偏振模式检验。

Result: 所有检验均未发现对广义相对论的显著偏离：残差符合噪声预期；低频与高频推断的最终质量与自旋一致；次主导多极矩幅度及偏振模式均与GR预测相符；整体结果支持纯真空GR。另两篇配套论文也显示>90%事件在90%可信水平下与GR一致。

Conclusion: 当前引力波观测数据（GWTC-4.0）仍与广义相对论高度一致，未发现确凿的新物理迹象；GR在强场、动力学引力区域继续保持其有效性。

Abstract: The worldwide LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA network of gravitational-wave (GW) detectors continues to increase in sensitivity, thus increasing the quantity and quality of the detected GW signals from compact binary coalescences. These signals allow us to perform ever-more sensitive tests of general relativity (GR) in the dynamical and strong-field regime of gravity. This paper is the first of three, where we present the results of a suite of tests of GR using the binary signals included in the fourth GW Transient Catalog (GWTC-4.0), i.e., up to and including the first part of the fourth observing run of the detectors (O4a). We restrict our analysis to the 91 confident signals, henceforth called events, that were measured by at least two detectors, and have false alarm rates $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$. These include 42 events from O4a. This first paper presents an overview of the methods, selection of events and GR tests, and serves as a guidemap for all three papers. Here we focus on the four general tests of consistency, where we find no evidence for deviations from our models. Specifically, for all the events considered, we find consistency of the residuals with noise. The final mass and final spin as inferred from the low- and high-frequency parts of the waveform are consistent with each other. We also find no evidence for deviations from the GR predictions for the amplitudes of subdominant GW multipole moments, or for non-GR modes of polarization. We thus find that GR, without new physics beyond it, is still consistent with these GW events. The results of the two additional papers in this trio also find overall consistency with vacuum GR, with more than 90% of the events being consistent with GR at the 90% credible level. While one of the ringdown analyses finds the GR value in the tails for its combined results, this may be due in part to catalog variance.

</details>

Zimmerman,L. Zimmermann,M. E. Zucker,J. Zweizig*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对GWTC-4.0中42个O4a及49个先前观测运行的致密双星并合事件，开展广义相对论（GR）的参数化检验与视线加速度约束，未发现偏离GR、Kerr黑洞四极矩或视线加速度的显著证据，更新了后牛顿系数、引力子质量等限制，结果支持GR。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验广义相对论在强引力场下的有效性，探索可能的新物理（如修正引力理论、引力子质量、非零视线加速度等）。

Method: 对GWTC-4.0中共91个高置信度引力波事件（42个来自O4a，49个来自先前运行），开展八类参数化GR检验，包括后牛顿参数偏差、自旋诱导四极矩偏离、传播色散/双折射效应及视线加速度建模。

Result: 90%以上事件在90%可信区间内兼容GR零偏差；后牛顿系数偏差限制提升1.2–5.5倍；引力子质量上限更新为mg ≤ 1.92×10⁻²³ eV/c²；未发现Kerr黑洞四极矩偏离或显著视线加速度。

Conclusion: 当前引力波数据强有力地支持广义相对论，所获多数偏离限制为迄今最优，暂无新物理迹象。

Abstract: In this second of three papers on tests of general relativity (GR) applied to the compact binary coalescence signals in the fourth Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog (GWTC-4.0), we present the results of the parameterized tests of GR and constraints on line-of-sight acceleration. We include events up to and including the first part of the fourth observing run (O4a) of the LIGO Virgo KAGRA detectors. As in the other two papers in this series, we restrict our analysis to the 42 confident signals, measured by at least two detectors, that have false alarm rates $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ from O4a, in addition to the 49 such events from previous observing runs. This paper focuses on the eight tests that constrain parameterized deviations from the expected GR (or unaccelerated) values. These include modifications of post-Newtonian (PN) parameters, spin-induced quadrupole moments different from those of a binary black hole, and possible dispersive or birefringent propagation effects. Overall, we find no evidence for physics beyond GR, for spin-induced quadrupole moments different from those of a Kerr black hole in GR, or for line of sight acceleration, with more than 90% of the events including the null result (no deviation) within their 90% credible intervals. We discuss possible systematics affecting the other events and tests, even though they are statistically not surprising, given noise. We improve the bounds on deviations from the GR PN coefficients by factors of 1.2-5.5 and provide illustrative translations to constraints on some modified theories. Also, we update the bound on the mass of the graviton, at 90% credibility, to $m_g \leq 1.92\times 10^{-23} \mathrm{eV}/c^2$. Thus, we see that GR holds, and many of the bounds on possible deviations derived from our events are the best to date.

</details>


### [64] [GWTC-4.0: Tests of General Relativity. III. Tests of the Remnants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19021)

Zimmermann,M. E. Zucker,J. Zweizig*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于GWTC-4.0引力波数据，首次对42个新事件及历史事件的并合残余（黑洞遗迹）开展七项广义相对论检验，包括环降信号与Kerr黑洞准正规模的一致性检验及后并合回声搜寻，整体结果与广义相对论一致，未发现显著偏离或回声证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验广义相对论在强引力场、动力学极端条件下的有效性，特别是黑洞并合后残余物的性质，如环降阶段是否符合Kerr黑洞的准正规模谱，以及是否存在广义相对论所不允许的后并合回声。

Method: 基于GWTC-4.0中42个O4a期及先前运行的高信噪比（≥2探测器、FAR ≤10⁻³ yr⁻¹）引力波事件，开展七项残余检验：三项聚焦环降信号（两项时域、一项频域）与Kerr黑洞理论预测的一致性；四项搜寻可能存在的后环降回声。采用似然乘积的层级联合分析，并通过自助法评估有限样本引起的统计涨落。

Result: 整体上，所有事件的残余行为与广义相对论预言一致；层级分析显示GR位于98.6%（99.3%）可信区边界，较GWTC-3.0有所提升，但该显著性在计入最新强事件GW250114后下降至92.2%（96.2%），表明此前微弱偏离可能源于样本有限；未发现任何回声证据。

Conclusion: 当前引力波数据对黑洞并合残余的观测与广义相对论高度一致，未提供其在强场下失效的可靠证据，也未支持存在新物理（如量子引力效应导致的回声）的迹象。

Abstract: This is the third paper of the set recording the results of the suite of tests of general relativity (GR) performed on the signals from the fourth Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog (GWTC-4.0), where we focus on the remnants of the binary mergers. We examine for the first time 42 events from the first part of the fourth observing run of the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA detectors, alongside events from the previous observation runs, restricting our analysis to the confident signals, which were measured in at least two detectors and that have false alarm rates $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$. This paper focuses on seven tests of the coalescence remnants. Three of these are tests of the ringdown and its consistency with the expected quasinormal mode spectrum of a Kerr black hole. Specifically, two tests analyze just the ringdown in the time domain, and the third test analyzes the entire signal in the frequency domain. Four tests allow for the existence of possible echoes arriving after the end of the ringdown, which are not expected in GR. We find overall consistency of the remnants with GR. When combining events by multiplying likelihoods (hierarchically), one analysis finds that the GR prediction lies at the boundary of the $98.6^{+1.4}_{-9.4}\%$ ($99.3^{+0.7}_{-4.5}\%$) credible region, an increase from $93.8^{+6.1}_{-20.0}\%$ ($94.9^{+4.4}_{-18.2}\%$) for GWTC-3.0. Here the ranges of values comes from bootstrapping to account for the finite number of events analyzed and suggest that some of the apparently significant deviation could be attributed to variance due to the finite catalog. Since the significance also decreases to 92.2% (96.2%) when including the more recent very loud event GW250114, there is no strong evidence for a GR deviation. We find no evidence for post-merger echoes in the events that were analyzed. (Abridged)

</details>


### [65] [Thermodynamic Analysis of Charged AdS Black Holes with Cloud of Strings in Einstein-Bumblebee Gravity via Tsallis Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19034)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在bumblebee引力框架下，被弦云包围的带电反德西特黑洞的热力学性质，发现弦云参数α、洛伦兹破缺参数ℓ和Tsallis非广延熵参数δ共同导致了比标准RN-AdS黑洞更丰富的相变与热力学行为，包括范德瓦尔斯型小-大黑洞相变、修正的临界量及焦耳-汤姆孙效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索洛伦兹对称性破缺、弦云背景和非广延熵对黑洞热力学（特别是相变与临界行为）的联合影响，以拓展对量子引力效应下黑洞热力学的理解。

Method: 基于bumblebee引力理论构建带电AdS黑洞度规，引入弦云模型与Tsallis熵框架；计算霍金温度、自由能、比热、状态方程、焦耳-汤姆孙系数等热力学量；分析相变、临界点、J-T膨胀及熵修正效应。

Result: 发现α和ℓ共同改变黑洞视界结构、霍金温度、自由能、比热及临界行为；系统呈现范德瓦尔斯型小-大黑洞相变；临界量被二者修正，普适比因洛伦兹破缺而改变；J-T反转曲线受参数偏移；Tsallis参数δ显著影响温度分布、稳定性区间、临界体积、自由能及霍金辐射稀疏性。

Conclusion: 弦云、洛伦兹破缺与非广延熵三者协同作用，使黑洞热力学结构远比标准RN-AdS黑洞复杂多样，为探测量子引力效应提供了新的热力学视角。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic properties of charged anti-de Sitter black holes surrounded by a cloud of strings in bumblebee gravity. In this framework, the cloud-of-strings parameter $α$ and the Lorentz-violating parameter $\ell$ modify the horizon structure, the Hawking temperature, the free energies, the specific heat, and the critical behavior in the extended phase-space description. We derive the corresponding equation of state and show that the system exhibits a small--large black-hole phase transition of Van der Waals type. In particular, the critical quantities are deformed by both the cloud of strings and the bumblebee background, while the universal ratio is explicitly altered by Lorentz symmetry breaking. We also examine the Joule--Thomson expansion and analyze the associated inversion and isenthalpic curves, showing how the deformation parameters shift the boundary between heating and cooling regions. In addition, we extend the thermodynamic analysis to a Tsallis entropy-based framework and show that the non-extensive parameter $δ$ significantly changes the temperature profile, stability windows, critical volume, free energies, and sparsity of Hawking radiation. Our results reveal that the combined effects of the string cloud, Lorentz violation, and non-extensive entropy lead to a substantially richer thermodynamic structure than that of the standard Reissner--Nordström--AdS black hole.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Lyra几何的Bianchi I型宇宙学模型，引入标量场，推导并分析其动力学方程，研究Lyra参数的演化约束及能量动量张量非守恒特性。

Result: 发现Lyra参数在早期宇宙中具有显著影响，随宇宙演化逐渐衰减，导致Lyra几何效应在当前宇宙中可忽略；同时揭示了Lyra几何下应力-能量张量不守恒的动力学表现。

Conclusion: Lyra几何为理解早期宇宙各向异性演化提供了有效框架，其参数具有自然的时间演化行为，支持从早期显著几何修正过渡到现今近似黎曼几何的宇宙图景。

Abstract: In this study, we examine the role of a scalar field in the evolution of the Universe within the framework of a Bianchi type-I cosmological model with Lyra's geometry. Previous research has explored the nonlinear spinor field in various anisotropic and isotropic cosmological models. In our current study, we and dynamical restrictions for Lyra parameters and violation of stress-energy tensor conservation within Lyra geometry. We shown that in considering cases behavior of Lyra's parameter corresponds to relative in?uence in early universe and absence of Lyra geometry in present universe.

### [67] [Black hole superradiance in Poincaré gauge theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19140)
*Sebastian Bahamonde,Jorge Gigante Valcarcel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在庞加莱规范理论框架下，时空挠率存在时黑洞超辐射现象，发现挠率使得狄拉克费米子可通过手征不对称性从旋转黑洞中提取能量，同时保持泡利不相容原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索广义相对论之外、引入时空挠率后对黑洞超辐射及能量提取机制的影响。

Method: 基于庞加莱规范理论，分析含挠率时空中的狄拉克费米子行为及其与旋转黑洞的相互作用。

Result: 证明挠率的存在使狄拉克费米子能通过手征不对称性实现从旋转黑洞的能量提取。

Conclusion: 挠率可作为新的几何自由度，拓展黑洞能量提取机制，并兼容量子统计原理（如泡利不相容原理）。

Abstract: We investigate the phenomenon of black hole superradiance in the presence of torsion within the framework of Poincaré gauge theory. In particular, in contrast to the classical approach of General Relativity, we show that the inclusion of torsion in the space-time geometry enables the energy extraction from rotating black holes by Dirac fermions via chiral asymmetry, while preserving the Pauli exclusion principle.

### [68] [When do real observers resolve de Sitter's imaginary problem?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18068)
*Ahmed Farag Ali*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文探讨了德西特时空欧几里得路径积分中普遍存在的虚相位如何阻碍吉本斯-霍金熵的直观态计数解释，并指出仅当观测者涨落与共形因子的负模一致时，才能消除该相位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 德西特路径积分中的普遍虚相位（i^{D+2}）妨碍对吉本斯-霍金熵作直接的状态计数解释，需厘清何种观测者能通过重组该相位恢复物理诠释。

Method: 基于Maldacena关于特定黑洞观测者可重整化该相位的思想，区分引力观测者与拓扑旁观者，分析红外有效作用量的度规无关性导致路径积分因子化，并以SU(3)规范理论和拓扑序为例检验条件。

Result: 发现信息承载的钟表是必要但不充分条件；唯有其涨落与共形因子负模一致的观测者，才属于能消除德西特虚相位的特殊类。

Conclusion: 德西特路径积分中的虚相位无法被任意信息处理能力的子系统消除；其是否可消取决于观测者动力学是否耦合于共形因子的不稳定模，这对量子宇宙学中观测者角色的理解具有根本意义。

Abstract: The universal phase $\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$ of the Euclidean de Sitter path integral obstructs a straightforward state-counting interpretation of the Gibbons--Hawking entropy. Building on Maldacena's proposal that specific black-hole observers can reorganize this phase, we derive a general constraint on when such ``real observers'' can succeed. By distinguishing \emph{gravitational observers} from \emph{topological spectators}, we show that any sector whose \emph{infrared effective} action is metric independent at the de Sitter saddle factorizes in the path integral, $\Ztot = \Zgrav^{(\text{obs})}\Ztop$, so the imaginary phase persists regardless of the sector's information-processing capabilities. Using confining $\SU(3)$ gauge theory and topological orders as examples, we demonstrate that an information-bearing clock is necessary but insufficient: only observers whose fluctuations share the negative modes of the conformal factor belong to the special class that can remove the de Sitter phase.

</details>


### [69] [End-of-the-World Singularities: The Good, the Bad, and the Heated-up](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18133)
*José Calderón-Infante,Gongrui Cheng,Alvaro Herráez,Thomas Van Riet*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了驱动标量场在场空间中趋向无限距离的余维一‘世界终结’曲率奇点，并将其与Gubser、Maldacena–Nuñez等判据进行对比；提出一个基于Ricci标量发散的新几何化判据，既兼容已有接受案例，也包容EFT弦和D7膜，并暗示距离猜想在有限温度下的推广可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验‘世界终结’曲率奇点是否应被排除，尤其在动态协边背景下；厘清不同奇点判据（Gubser、Maldacena–Nuñez）的适用范围与局限性；为无限距离行为与有效理论失效之间的关系提供更普适的几何判据。

Method: 系统比较Gubser的势能判据、Horizon判据及Maldacena–Nuñez判据；分析模空间流、Klebanov–Tseytlin/Strassler解、EFT弦、D7膜及黑Dp膜等典型例子；构造一致的弦论上提（uplift）；提出并验证基于Ricci标量发散的新判据；研究有限温度下场空间距离与温度的指数关系。

Result: 模空间流满足Gubser势能判据和（部分）Maldacena–Nuñez判据，且可一致上提至弦论背景，故不应被排除；EFT弦与D7膜虽有良好UV补全却违反Gubser势能判据；新提出的Ricci标量判据能统一涵盖上述所有案例，但仍拒绝IIA强耦合‘世界终结’奇点；黑Dp膜约化显示温度与场空间距离呈指数关系，暗示距离猜想的有限温推广。

Conclusion: ‘世界终结’奇点不应一概而论地排除；需采用更精细的几何判据（如Ricci标量发散）来刻画无限距离极限下的EFT失效；该框架支持距离猜想向有限温度和动态协边情境自然延拓。

Abstract: We revisit codimension-one End-of-the-World curvature singularities that drive scalars to infinite distance in field-space and have appeared in the context of dynamical cobordisms. We confront them with Gubser's horizon and potential criteria and with the Maldacena--Nuñez criterion. Moduli-space flows do not admit a near-extremal horizon generalization. Still, they satisfy Gubser's potential criterion and, in representative string realizations, the Maldacena--Nuñez criterion in ten dimensions. Together with an explicit uplift of this type of solution to a consistent string theory background, this suggests that such singularities should not be discarded. For flows with non-trivial scalar potential, we argue that the fate of the singularity is tied to the infinite-distance limit probed near the singularity. The Klebanov--Tseytlin and Klebanov--Strassler solutions illustrate that a modification that obstructs or modifies the field excursion should not be understood as a UV-resolution of the original singularity. We show that EFT strings and D7-branes fail Gubser's potential criterion despite having a sensible UV completion. Motivated by this, and inspired by dynamical cobordisms, we propose a novel criterion that bounds the divergence of the Ricci scalar as the flow explores infinite distance in field-space. Our criterion can be viewed as a geometrization Gubser's one that, while capturing all examples accepted by the latter, also admits EFT strings and D7-branes. Both criteria reject the massive Type IIA strong coupling End-of-the-World singularity. Finally, we analyze black D$p$-branes reduced to codimension one as representatives of flows that admit near-extremal generalizations, and find an exponential relation between temperature and field-space distance. This suggests a finite-temperature extension of the Distance Conjecture for dynamical cobordisms.

</details>


### [70] [The Resolved Elliptic Genus and the D1-D5 CFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18138)
*Marcel R. R. Hughes,Masaki Shigemori*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了D1-D5 CFT在T^4上的新超对称指数——解析椭圆亏格（REG），作为标准修正椭圆亏格（MEG）的单参数推广；基于Schur-Weyl对偶的新形式框架，通过超荷受精确边缘算子变形后的超选择规则，构造REG以仅对可混合的对称性扇区求和；REG在黑洞阈值以下与超引力高度一致（而MEG在此区域几乎平凡），阈值以上则主导于传统MEG不可见的黑洞微态分布扇区；该新形式与REG有望助力黑洞微态结构研究，尤其关联‘fortuity’纲领。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决标准修正椭圆亏格（MEG）在黑洞阈值以下几乎平凡、无法有效刻画BPS态提升及黑洞微态分布的问题，亟需一个更精细的超对称指数来揭示对称性扇区层面的微态结构。

Method: 发展基于Schur-Weyl对偶的自由对称 orbifold CFT 新形式框架，将希尔伯特空间按对称性扇区分解；分析受精确边缘算子变形的超荷作用，提出控制BPS态提升的超选择规则；据此仅对满足该规则的扇区求和，构造解析椭圆亏格（REG）。

Result: 成功定义并构造了REG，其在黑洞阈值以下与超引力预言高度一致，显著优于MEG；在阈值以上，REG能分辨并分布于多个传统MEG不可见的对称性扇区中的黑洞微态；验证了新形式框架对理解微态混合机制的有效性。

Conclusion: REG与所发展的Schur-Weyl对偶形式框架为研究D1-D5系统中黑洞微态的精细结构提供了强有力新工具，尤其可能推动‘fortuity’纲领在CFT中实现对黑洞微观起源的深入理解。

Abstract: This paper is a follow-up to the short paper arXiv:2509.19425, greatly expanding the discussion with examples and providing derivations and justifications of results presented there.
  We introduce a new supersymmetry index for the D1-D5 CFT on $T^4$, which we call the resolved elliptic genus (REG). It is a one-parameter generalisation of the standard supersymmetry index, the modified elliptic genus (MEG), and arises naturally in the free symmetric orbifold description of the theory within a new formalism, based on Schur-Weyl duality, that we develop. In this formalism, the Hilbert space of the symmetric orbifold CFT is decomposed into symmetry sectors in which the structure of the states contributing to the MEG is transparent. By examining the action of the supercharge deformed by an exactly marginal operator on the relevant symmetry algebra, we propose a superselection rule governing the lifting process of BPS states, and use it to construct the REG by summing only over those symmetry sectors that can mix according to this rule. The REG exhibits detailed agreement between the CFT and supergravity below the black-hole threshold, a regime in which the MEG is essentially trivial. Above the threshold, the REG is dominated by black-hole microstates, which are now distributed amongst distinct sectors that are invisible to the MEG. We expect both the new formalism and the REG to provide useful new tools for studying the structure of black-hole microstates. In particular, we comment on their possible relevance to the fortuity program for understanding black-hole microstates within CFT.

Most importantly, the moment bootstrap reveals new features in previously unexplored regions of the bootstrap landscape. The lower bounds on moment variables exhibit two continuous families of kinks persisting across $2 < d < 6$, reflecting nontrivial spectral reorganizations connected to underlying operator decoupling phenomena. These results demonstrate that moment variables uncover bootstrap solutions and collective structures that are difficult to access within traditional numerical approaches.

We describe and solve a complete classification of all possible generalised Schwarzian theories, defined by integrals over any Virasoro coadjoint orbit, including new classes of theories with qualitatively novel features. The classification of coadjoint orbits coincides with the moduli space of constant positive curvature two-dimensional Lorentzian geometries, and the associated Schwarzian theories govern associated wavefunctions in asymptotically near-dS$_2$ gravity (Jackiw-Teitelboim gravity in particular). A recent proposal by Kurlyand and Tseytlin, based on the Pasti-Sorokin-Tonin formulation, resolves this issue for a special class of backgrounds including the $AdS_5\times S^5$ vacuum by introducing a topological term required for consistency, yielding a non-vanishing on-shell value in agreement with holography. We test the proposal on non-trivial solutions such as the Lunin-Maldacena background and the $AdS_4$ $S$-fold solution, and find agreement with the corresponding lower-dimensional gauged supergravity on-shell actions and thereby with the expected holographic observables. Our results place direct holographic comparisons within the ten-dimensional Type IIB framework on firmer ground.

*Diego Gallego,J. Bayron Orjuela-Quintana*

TL;DR: 本文研究了由弦紧致化启发的指数型双场精质模型（含膨胀子和轴子）在弯曲弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃尔克（FLRW）宇宙中的动力学行为，结合动力系统分析、解析近似与数值模拟，发现空间曲率与非测地轨迹虽理论上可分别支持加速膨胀，但在含辐射与物质的实际宇宙中无法共存；观测数据给出势能斜率上限λ≲0.75（95%置信水平），表明即使在最简多场弯曲宇宙框架下，持续晚期加速仍需平坦势能，从而延续了宇宙加速与量子引力预期之间的张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由弦理论紧致化自然导出的指数型双场精质模型包含耦合于弯曲场流形的膨胀子与轴子；同时，空间曲率拓展宇宙相空间并可能影响晚期宇宙演化，亟需系统考察其联合效应。

Method: 在含辐射、物质与空间曲率的FLRW背景下，对最小双场指数势系统开展完整动力系统分类，并辅以解析近似与数值积分，识别并分析各类不动点及其稳定性，特别关注非测地轨迹、标度-曲率不动点及含背景流体下的相空间结构。

Result: 1) 标量主导极限下非测地轨迹可在陡峭势上维持加速膨胀；2) 弯曲宇宙中存在标度-曲率不动点，理论上可降低加速要求；3) 但二者位于不同不变流形，在含背景流体时无法共存——不存在开放参数区域内的非测地标度不动点；4) 在可观测的解冻区，轴子不跟踪背景流体，曲率迅速压低，演化退化为有效单场；5) 曲率效应与标量动力学存在简并，限制其独立影响；6) 观测拟合给出势能斜率上限λ≲0.75（95% CL）。

Conclusion: 即使在含空间曲率的最简双场精质模型中，实现持续晚期加速仍依赖足够平坦的势能，因此宇宙加速现象与量子引力对陡峭势的天然偏好之间仍存在根本性张力，该张力未被多场或曲率效应所缓解。

Abstract: Exponential quintessence models motivated by string compactifications naturally involve both a dilatonic scalar and its axionic partner evolving on a curved field space, while spatial curvature enlarges the cosmological phase space and may affect late-time dynamics. We perform a systematic analysis of the minimal two-field exponential system in a curved FLRW background including radiation and matter components, combining a complete dynamical systems classification with analytical approximations and numerical integration. In the scalar-dominated limit, non-geodesic trajectories can sustain accelerated expansion on steep potentials, and in curved universes a scaling-curvature fixed point can in principle soften the requirements for acceleration. However, we show that these mechanisms arise in distinct invariant manifolds and cannot be simultaneously realized in the presence of a background fluid: no non-geodesic scaling fixed point exists within an open region of parameter space. As a consequence, in the observationally viable thawing regime the axion does not track the background fluid and spatial curvature becomes dynamically subdominant, leading to an effectively single-field evolution. We further identify a degeneracy between curvature effects and scalar-field dynamics that limits their independent impact on late-time cosmology. Confronting the model with current cosmological background data (Planck 2018 distance priors, Pantheon+, BAO, and cosmic chronometers), we obtain an upper bound $λ\lesssim 0.75$ (95 percent CL) on the potential slope. Our results demonstrate that even in the minimal multifield setup with spatial curvature, sustained late-time acceleration requires a sufficiently flat potential, so that the tension between cosmic acceleration and quantum gravity expectations persists within this framework.

</details>

Abstract: We study soft emission in QED during scattering of Faddeev-Kulish dressed states. We focus on explicit processes that allow the dependence of the soft factors on the hard particles' momenta and total angular momenta to be displayed clearly. We argue that the dressings remove the infrared divergences in hard amplitudes order by order in perturbation theory, effectively regulating the contributions from virtual soft photons at the scale $E_d$. Essentially, the Faddeev-Kulish hard amplitudes become equivalent to the infrared-finite part of the corresponding Fock-basis amplitudes. Finally, tree-level soft-photon emission is found to be suppressed once the dressings are extended to subleading order in the soft-momentum expansion, as prescribed in recent work by Choi and Akhoury.

Abstract: The M-theoretic Emergence Proposal claims that all of the terms in the low-energy action arise from quantum effects. After reviewing the current status of this proposal, we focus on four-dimensional compactifications with $N=2$ supersymmetry, where kinetic terms are encoded in topological string amplitudes, such as the prepotential $F_0$. Evidence for the emergence of such terms was provided recently, where in particular it was shown that the classical cubic term in $F_0$ can be obtained by integrating out the light towers of states in the M-theory limit, using a novel regularization of the infinite sum over Gopakumar/Vafa invariants. Moreover, we establish a correspondence between the spontaneous breaking of an emergent PT symmetry of the dilatation operator and the fundamental spacetime PT symmetry of the underlying gauge theory. In the vicinity of EPs, the resulting non-Hermitian dynamics produces logarithmic scaling behavior in correlation functions, characteristic of logarithmic conformal field theories. Method: 将标量扰动的主方程（双合流Heun方程）映射到Nekrasov-Shatashvili极限下的量子Seiberg-Witten曲线，并利用其自由能导出的量子化条件非微扰求解准正规模频率。

Result: 解析结果精确复现质量为零场的数值基准；成功刻画了大质量探针在严格极值极限下的准共振行为。

Conclusion: 量子规范理论的几何方法可有效描述极值黑洞的线性扰动谱，为引力与规范理论的深刻联系提供了新证据。

Abstract: We study the neutral scalar perturbations of asymptotically flat extremal Reissner-Nordström black holes via the quantum geometry of $\mathcal{N}=2$ $\mathrm{SU(2)}$ gauge theory with $N_f=2$ flavors. The master equation, given by a double confluent Heun equation, is mapped to the quantum Seiberg-Witten curve in the Nekrasov-Shatashvili limit. We compute the quasinormal mode frequencies non-perturbatively using the quantization condition derived from the Nekrasov-Shatashvili free energy. Our analytical results accurately reproduce the numerical benchmarks for massless fields, and capture the quasi-resonance behavior of massive probes at the strict extremal limit.

</details>

### [89] [Decay and structure of heavy flavour](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18098)
*Stefan Groote,Arpan Chatterjee,Maria Naeem*

<details>

Method: 采用流代数方法结合张量不变量处理粲重子衰变；引入非局域场算符解释内在粲夸克；将非局域Nambu-Jona-Lasinio模型与相对论Faddeev方法结合描述强子态；使用螺旋度方法计算电弱辐射修正。

Result: 揭示了SELEX与LHCb在内在粲夸克观测上的差异可由非局域算符解释；建立了适用于强子谱与衰变的非局域NJL-Faddeev框架；指出Higgs→4ℓ中全同粒子与质量效应不可忽略；表明中子β衰变和极化W衰变中存在可观测的新物理与辐射修正效应。

Conclusion: 强子物理需融合非局域性、对称性分析与多体方法；若干开放问题（如内在粲机制确认、CP破坏长程主导验证、非局域QCD有效理论构建）有待COST行动进一步协同攻关。

Abstract: In accordance to the aim of the constituing meeting of the COST action CA24159 ``Structure and Spectroscopy of Hadrons Research Project'' to introduce the different groups to the action, in this talk we give an overview over the subjects dealt with by the working group in Tartu related to hadron physics. We deal with the production and the nonleptonic decays of charmed baryons in the framework of the current algebra approach in terms of tensor invariants and explain how this approach can be used to approach CP violation via long distance effects in rescattering. New physics effects can be even seen in the classical neutron beta decay, but the helicity approach used here is also useful for e.g.\ calculating first order electroweak radiative corrections to the decay of the polarised $W$ boson. Identical particle and mass effects are seen in the Higgs decay into four leptons of the same type. The second main part starts with indications for the intrinsic charm mechanism, explaining the discrepancy between the results of SELEX and LHCb. The solution offered here is valid only if one considers nonlocal field operators. The nonlocal extension of the Nambu--Jona-Lasinio model, derived directly from QCD and combined with the relativistic Faddeev approach, allows for the description of hadronic states. We conclude by presenting open questions to the action.

### [90] [Phasing out Dark Matter Isocurvature with Thermal Misalignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18132)
*Brian Batell,Akshay Ghalsasi,Subhajit Ghosh,Mudit Rai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的标量暗物质产生机制——热错位机制，通过热浴粒子的微弱耦合诱导标量场在辐射主导早期获得大场值，从而动态实现错位；该机制能自然抑制与高能标暴胀相关的暗物质等熵扰动信号，为等熵安全的标量暗物质提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准错位机制中轻标量暗物质因暴胀量子涨落会产生成分强烈的等熵扰动，受到CMB观测的严格限制；本文旨在探索一种能规避该限制的新机制。

Method: 基于有限温度场论构建热错位机制模型，分析热浴诱导的有限温势对标量场演化的影响，并计算其背景零模与超视界扰动之间的相位偏移，进而推导暗物质密度扰动和等熵谱。

Result: 热错位机制可显著压低最终暗物质密度对比度，从而自然抑制等熵扰动功率谱，使轻标量暗物质在高能标暴胀下仍满足CMB等熵约束。

Conclusion: 热错位是一种新颖且普适的标量暗物质产生机制，能有效解决标准错位机制中的等熵问题，拓展了轻标量暗物质的可行参数空间。

Abstract: Thermal misalignment provides an alternative to the standard misalignment mechanism for the cosmological production of scalar dark matter. In this framework, feeble couplings to particles in the thermal bath generate a finite-temperature potential that drives the scalar towards large field values early in the radiation era, dynamically inducing the misalignment before the onset of scalar oscillations. As a result, the relic abundance is controlled primarily by particle masses and couplings rather than the initial field value. As a light spectator field, the scalar acquires inflationary fluctuations that are uncorrelated with the adiabatic curvature mode, generically sourcing isocurvature perturbations. We show that, unlike standard misalignment, where light scalars are strongly constrained by cosmic microwave background bounds on dark matter isocurvature for high-scale inflation, thermal misalignment can naturally suppress the isocurvature signal. This occurs through a novel late-time phase offset between the background zero mode and the superhorizon perturbations, which reduces the final dark matter density contrast. Thermal misalignment therefore provides a new and generic route to isocurvature-safe scalar dark matter.

*Massimo Cipressi,Kevin Langhoff,Toby Opferkuch*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: beamstrahlung 效应可大幅增强对重矢量共振态的探测灵敏度，实现等效的宽范围质心能量扫描。

Conclusion: beamstrahlung 并非单纯缺陷，而是可被利用的新物理探测新途径，尤其适用于宽质量范围的共振态搜索。

Abstract: We explore the potential of future high-energy lepton colliders to probe heavy vector resonances. At wakefield colliders, intense beam-beam interactions produce radiation, called beamstrahlung, which redistributes luminosity from the nominal energy across a broad spectrum of lower collision energies. We show that this effect, conventionally viewed as a drawback, dramatically enhances sensitivity to resonances by effectively scanning a wide range of center-of-mass energies. We present projections for a benchmark scenario of a heavy kinetically mixed $Z'$.

### [93] [Two-Component Dark Matter in the Type-I 2HDM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18158)
*Patricio Escalona,Jacinto P. Neto,M. J. Neves,Camila Ramos,David Suarez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在I型双Higgs二重态模型中研究了一个由实标量s和Dirac费米子χ组成的双组分暗物质模型，利用Z4对称性与运动学条件保证其稳定性，并通过Higgs-门户耦合和Yukawa相互作用与可见物质耦合；通过参数扫描并结合理论约束与实验限制（如暗物质丰度、希格斯不可见衰变、直接探测、电弱精度观测量等），发现尽管存在满足所有暗物质约束的参数区域，但对撞机限制显著压缩了标量暗物质的允许质量范围，尤其在亚TeV区域与暗物质现象学偏好产生张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决单组分暗物质模型难以同时满足多种实验约束的问题，探索双组分暗物质在扩展希格斯扇区（如2HDM）中的可行性及 phenomenological 特征。

Method: 构建基于Z4对称性的两组分暗物质模型（实标量s + Dirac费米子χ），纳入Higgs-portal与Yukawa相互作用；数值求解玻尔兹曼方程以计算热冻结产额，包含湮灭、转化与半湮灭过程；在多维参数空间（质量、混合角、门户耦合）进行全局扫描，并施加理论自洽性（可微扰性、真空稳定性）与实验约束。

Result: 存在满足全部暗物质观测与实验约束（包括Planck测得的遗迹丰度、LHC的Higgs不可见衰变上限、XENON等直接探测限、S参数等电弱精度数据）的参数区域；但LHC对希格斯耦合与新标量粒子的搜索强烈限制标量暗物质质量，尤其在<1 TeV区间，导致与暗物质唯象学偏好的区域出现明显张力。

Conclusion: 该双组分框架在理论上可行且可缓解部分单组分模型的紧张关系，但当前对撞机限制已对轻标量暗物质构成严峻挑战，未来高亮度LHC或下一代对撞机将是检验该模型的关键。

Abstract: We investigate a two-component dark matter scenario in the type-I two-Higgs-doublet model. The dark sector contains a real scalar $s$ and a Dirac fermion $χ$, whose stability is ensured by a $Z_4$ symmetry together with kinematic conditions. The scalar interacts with the visible sector through Higgs-portal couplings, while the fermion interacts with the scalar via Yukawa interactions. In this framework, we analyze the thermal freeze-out production of both candidates, accounting for annihilation, conversion, and semi-annihilation processes. A comprehensive scan over the multidimensional parameter space is performed in terms of physical masses, mixing angles, and portal couplings, imposing theoretical requirements such as perturbativity and vacuum stability. We confront the model with current experimental constraints, including the observed relic abundance, invisible Higgs decays, direct detection limits on spin-independent scattering cross sections, and electroweak precision observables. We find that viable regions of parameter space can satisfy all dark matter constraints, but collider bounds strongly constrain the scalar sector, narrowing the allowed regions and creating tension with those favored by dark matter phenomenology, particularly in the sub-TeV mass regime.

Abstract: The meV mass range has emerged as a focal point in axion physics, where advances in theory, cosmology, astrophysics, and experimental techniques converge. Axions in this mass range are theoretically well motivated, can arise in ultraviolet-complete models, and can have significant cosmological impacts as dark matter or dark radiation. In parallel, their efficient production in stellar and supernova environments provides powerful astrophysical probes. Here, we provide a comprehensive overview of meV axions across these domains, highlighting both established results and open questions. We discuss the theoretical underpinnings of meV axions, their cosmological and astrophysical signatures, and the diverse experimental strategies -- ranging from helioscopes and haloscopes to quasiparticle systems and large-volume Cherenkov detectors -- that aim to explore this regime. The convergence of these approaches emphasizes the pivotal role of the meV mass range for axion discovery in the coming years, identifying meV axions as a key probe for testing beyond-Standard-Model physics. This review document is the direct outcome of the discussions at the dedicated workshop "The meV Mass Axion Frontier: Challenges and Opportunities", held at Laboratori Nazionali di Frascati (IT) on 27--28 October 2025, and organized by the EU funded COST Action "Cosmic WISPers in the Dark Universe: Theory, astrophysics, and experiments" (CA21106, https://www.cost.eu/actions/CA21106). Its aim is to provide an overview of current efforts in meV axion research, their motivations, and the research goals that animate the community involved in this search.

### [96] [The impact of prescriptions in phenomenological extractions of Transverse Momentum Dependent distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19088)

TL;DR: 本文研究了CSS方法中phenomenological prescriptions对横动量分布（TMDs）全局提取的影响，发现不同b*处方在低能Drell-Yan数据拟合中表现相似，但在中等横动量区域差异显著，影响高能过程预测，揭示b*处方是CSS框架中不可忽略的理论不确定性来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigate the impact of phenomenological prescriptions in the Collins-Soper-Sterman (CSS) approach for global extractions of Transverse Momentum Distributions (TMDs). We show that fits to low-energy Drell-Yan data with different choices of $b_*$ prescription yield equally good agreement with data and similar TMDs at small partonic transverse momentum. In contrast, sizable differences emerge at intermediate transverse momentum region, significantly affecting the predictions for high-energy Drell-Yan processes. Our results demonstrate that the $b_*$ prescription represents an intrinsic source of theoretical uncertainty in the CSS approach, introducing systematic effects that influence TMD extractions and their interpretation. At the same time, our analysis emphasizes the interplay between data at different energy scales in assessing the effect of phenomenological prescriptions in TMD fits adopting the CSS framework.

### [97] [Nuclear transverse momentum dependent gluon density at low $x$ and inclusive soft hadron production in proton-lead collisions at LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18312)
